============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK13)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (independent of `t`):
\[
f(A)= -0.23236613283613416\,A + 0.395876449251558\,\sin(0.5265654762365851\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of `t` for all `t`, and (ii) reproduce a genuine sine-in-`A` term plus a linear-in-`A` term, with no extra dependence (no polynomials-only, no abs, no logs, no exponentials, etc.), unless those extra parts can be set to zero by parameters.

Now check each candidate.

1. Polynomial in \(A\) + constant + \(c6 e^{A c7} e^{c8 t}\). To remove `t`, need \(c6=0\) or \(c8=0\) and also kill the \(e^{A c7}\) mismatch; setting \(c6=0\) leaves a pure polynomial/constant in \(A\), cannot equal linear+sine for all \(A\). No.
2. Pure polynomial/constant in \(A\). Cannot equal linear+sine for all \(A\). No.
3. Pure polynomial/constant in \(A\). No.
4. Polynomial + \(c4|A|\). Still no sine; also non-smooth at 0 unless \(c4=0\). No.
5. Polynomial in \(A\). No.
6. Polynomial in \(A\). No.
7. Linear in \(A\) only. Cannot produce sine term. No.
8. Has \(t\)-dependent rational terms and \(|A|\). To remove `t` need those coefficients 0; then becomes quadratic/linear/abs/constant, no sine. No.
9. Entirely scaled by \((c1+t)^{-1}\) with \(t\) in numerators; cannot become `t`-independent for all \(t\) unless all coefficients zero, yielding 0, not GT. No.
10. Polynomial/constant + \(c6\exp(c7\exp(A c8 t))\) (strong \(t\) dependence). Setting \(c6=0\) leaves polynomial/constant, no sine. No.
11. \(A\) terms + \(A*c2*\cos(c3\log(A c4+1))\). No way to turn \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\) into \(\sin(kA)\) for all \(A\) by constants. No.
12. Has explicit \(t\)-dependent fractions and \(\log(c5 e^{A c6}+1)\). Killing \(t\)-dependence forces those coefficients to 0, leaving at best quadratic/linear, no sine. No.
13. Has \(t\)-dependent term and \(c7\exp(c8\exp(A c9))\). Even if set \(c7=0\) and \(t\)-term 0, remaining is polynomial/abs, no sine. No.
14. \(A^2\) + \(A\) + \(t\)-dependent rational. Remove \(t\) by setting \(c2=0\), leaving quadratic+linear, no sine. No.
15. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 (A c2+1)^{c3}\). This is algebraic/power, not sine. No.
16. Includes \(A*c3*e^{c4 t}\) and \(1/(c7+t)\). Remove by setting \(c3=0,c6=0\); left quadratic/linear/constant, no sine. No.
17. Has \(A*c2(c3+t)^{c4}\). To remove `t`, need \(c2=0\) (or \(c4=0\) making it constant factor, still just linear term). Either way no sine. No.
18. Has \(A*c2\log(A c3+1)\cos(c4 t)\) and \(|A|^2\). Remove `t` by \(c2=0\) or force \(\cos(c4 t)\) constant for all \(t\) (only if \(c4=0\), then term is \(A\log(\cdot)\), not sine). No.
19. Similar to 17 plus \(|A|^2\). No sine. No.
20. Polynomial/constant in \(A\). No.
21. Rational in \(A\) plus \(|A|\) plus \(t\)-dependent rational. Removing extras yields polynomial/rational, no sine. No.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK13)

GT: -c0*A + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can exactly match the Ground Truth:

**GT: -0.23237*A + 0.39588*sin(0.52657*A)**

This is a function of A only (no t dependence). It contains a linear term in A and a sin(A) term.

Let me analyze the key structural requirement: The GT has a **sinusoidal component** `sin(c*A)`. Since sin is not a polynomial, exponential, logarithmic, or rational function, candidates must either contain sin/cos terms or contain functions that can exactly reproduce sin behavior.

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidates 1-10, 20:** These are polynomials in A (possibly with exp or t terms). Polynomials cannot exactly equal sin(A) for all A. Setting exp coefficients to 0 leaves only polynomials. **NO MATCH** for all pure polynomial candidates.

Let me check each more carefully:

**Candidate 1:** A³c0 + A*c1 + ... + c6*exp(A*c7)*exp(c8*t). Setting c8=0 gives exp(A*c7) term, but exp ≠ sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 2-7, 20:** Pure polynomials in A. Cannot match sin(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** Has A², A, Abs(A), 1/(c+t) terms. Setting t-dependent terms to 0 and using A≥0 (Abs(A)=A): becomes A²c0 + A*(c1+c4) + c7. Polynomial, no sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9:** All terms have 1/(c1+t), so t-dependent. Cannot be t-independent unless denominator is constant, but then it's polynomial in A. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** Has exp(c7*exp(A*c8*t)). Setting c8=0 makes it exp(c7), a constant. Remaining: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*cos(c3*log(A*c4+1)). This has cos(c3*log(A*c4+1)), not sin(c*A). These are different functions. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 12-50:** Let me focus on candidates with sin, cos, tanh, or log(exp()) that could potentially produce sin:

**Candidate 25, 26:** Contains log(c8*exp(A*c9)+1) which is a softplus, not sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 30:** Has tanh(c5*t+c6). Setting coefficients to make t-independent: tanh(c6) is constant. Remaining: A*c0/(A*c1+1)^5 + A*c2/(A+c3) + const. Rational functions, not sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 35:** Has exp(c8*cos(A*c9)). This is exp(cos(A)), not sin(A). Cannot match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 42:** Has tanh, not sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** No A dependence possible to match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** Has A^c4 * c5. Could this work? Still no sin term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** Has A^c5 * c6. No sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** A^c0*c1*log(c2*t+1) + c3/(c4+t) + c5*t^c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8)+1). Has log(exp()) softplus, not sin. **NO MATCH**

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates contain a sin() or equivalent function that could reproduce sin(c*A). The GT fundamentally requires a sinusoidal basis function, which is absent from all candidates.
